class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Enlargement_of_the_European_Union" title="Enlargement of the European Union">Enlargement of the European Union</a>, <a href="/wiki/Future_enlargement_of_the_European_Union" title="Future enlargement of the European Union">Future enlargement of the European Union</a>, <a href="/wiki/Federal_Europe" class="mw-redirect" title="Federal Europe">Federal Europe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eurosphere" title="Eurosphere">Eurosphere</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eurasian_Union" class="mw-redirect" title="Eurasian Union">Eurasian Union</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Enlargement_of_the_Eurasian_Economic_Union" title="Enlargement of the Eurasian Economic Union">Enlargement of the Eurasian Economic Union</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:282px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Further_European_Union_Enlargement.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Further_European_Union_Enlargement.svg/280px-Further_European_Union_Enlargement.svg.png" width="280" height="214" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Further_European_Union_Enlargement.svg/420px-Further_European_Union_Enlargement.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Further_European_Union_Enlargement.svg/560px-Further_European_Union_Enlargement.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="680" data-file-height="520" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Further_European_Union_Enlargement.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/De_jure" title="De jure">De jure</a> status of possible <a href="/wiki/Future_enlargement_of_the_European_Union" title="Future enlargement of the European Union">future enlargement of the European Union</a>:<span style="margin:0px; padding-bottom:1px; font-size:90%; text-align:left; display:block;"><span style="border:#3F48CC solid 1px;; background-color:#3F48CC; color:#3F48CC">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</span>&#160;Current member states</span> <span style="margin:0px; padding-bottom:1px; font-size:90%; text-align:left; display:block;"><span style="border:#FF1493 solid 1px;; background-color:#FF1493; color:#FF1493">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</span>&#160;Member state which has given notice of its intent to <a href="/wiki/Withdrawal_from_the_European_Union" title="Withdrawal from the European Union">withdraw from the EU</a>: <a href="/wiki/Brexit" title="Brexit">United Kingdom</a></span><span style="margin:0px; padding-bottom:1px; font-size:90%; text-align:left; display:block;"><span style="border:#00BFFF solid 1px;; background-color:#00BFFF; color:#00BFFF">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</span>&#160;Candidates: <a href="/wiki/Accession_of_Albania_to_the_European_Union" title="Accession of Albania to the European Union">Albania</a>, <a href="/wiki/Accession_of_Macedonia_to_the_European_Union" title="Accession of Macedonia to the European Union">Macedonia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Accession_of_Montenegro_to_the_European_Union" title="Accession of Montenegro to the European Union">Montenegro</a>, <a href="/wiki/Accession_of_Serbia_to_the_European_Union" title="Accession of Serbia to the European Union">Serbia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Accession_of_Turkey_to_the_European_Union" title="Accession of Turkey to the European Union">Turkey</a><sup id="cite_ref-status1_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-status1-57">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup></span> <span style="margin:0px; padding-bottom:1px; font-size:90%; text-align:left; display:block;"><span style="border:#86FDF1 solid 1px;; background-color:#86FDF1; color:#86FDF1">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</span>&#160;Potential candidates that have applied for membership: <a href="/wiki/Accession_of_Bosnia_and_Herzegovina_to_the_European_Union" title="Accession of Bosnia and Herzegovina to the European Union">Bosnia and Herzegovina</a></span> <span style="margin:0px; padding-bottom:1px; font-size:90%; text-align:left; display:block;"><span style="border:#FFF200 solid 1px;; background-color:#FFF200; color:#FFF200">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</span>&#160;Potential candidates that have not applied for membership: <a href="/wiki/Accession_of_Kosovo_to_the_European_Union" title="Accession of Kosovo to the European Union">Kosovo*</a> (<i><a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Kosovo" title="International recognition of Kosovo">status disputed</a></i>).<sup id="cite_ref-status1_57-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-status1-57">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup></span> <span style="margin:0px; padding-bottom:1px; font-size:90%; text-align:left; display:block;"><span style="border:DarkOrange solid 1px;; background-color:DarkOrange; color:DarkOrange">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</span>&#160;States that have frozen or withdrawn their applications: <a href="/wiki/Accession_of_Iceland_to_the_European_Union" class="mw-redirect" title="Accession of Iceland to the European Union">Iceland</a> (frozen), <a href="/wiki/Norway%E2%80%93European_Union_relations" title="Norway\xe2\x80\x93European Union relations">Norway</a> (withdrawn), <a href="/wiki/Switzerland%E2%80%93European_Union_relations" title="Switzerland\xe2\x80\x93European Union relations">Switzerland</a> (withdrawn)</span> <span style="margin:0px; padding-bottom:1px; font-size:90%; text-align:left; display:block;"><span style="border:#48cc3f solid 1px;; background-color:#48cc3f; color:#48cc3f">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</span>&#160;States which have both ratified an <a href="/wiki/European_Union_Association_Agreement" title="European Union Association Agreement">EU Association Agreement</a> and have had their European perspective for membership explicitly recognised by the EU: <a href="/wiki/Georgia%E2%80%93European_Union_relations" title="Georgia\xe2\x80\x93European Union relations">Georgia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Moldova%E2%80%93European_Union_relations" title="Moldova\xe2\x80\x93European Union relations">Moldova</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ukraine%E2%80%93European_Union_relations" title="Ukraine\xe2\x80\x93European Union relations">Ukraine</a> (members of <a href="/wiki/Deep_and_Comprehensive_Free_Trade_Area" title="Deep and Comprehensive Free Trade Area">DCFTA</a>)</span></div></div></div>\n<p>There is no fixed end to the process of integration. The discussion on the possible final political shape or configuration of the European Union is sometimes referred to as the debate on the <b>finalit\xc3\xa9 politique</b> (French for \xe2\x80\x9cpolitical purpose\xe2\x80\x9d).<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Integration and <a href="/wiki/Enlargement_of_the_European_Union" title="Enlargement of the European Union">enlargement of the European Union</a> are major issues in the politics of Europe, each at European, national and local level. Integration may conflict with national <a href="/wiki/Sovereignty" title="Sovereignty">sovereignty</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cultural_identity" title="Cultural identity">cultural identity</a>, and is opposed by <a href="/wiki/Euroscepticism" title="Euroscepticism">eurosceptics</a>. To the east of the European Union, the countries of <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarus</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan" title="Kazakhstan">Kazakhstan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> launched the creation of the <a href="/wiki/Eurasian_Union" class="mw-redirect" title="Eurasian Union">Eurasian Union</a> in the year 2015, which was subsequently joined by <a href="/wiki/Armenia" title="Armenia">Armenia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kyrgyzstan" title="Kyrgyzstan">Kyrgyzstan</a>. Other states in the region, such as <a href="/wiki/Moldova" title="Moldova">Moldova</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tajikistan" title="Tajikistan">Tajikistan</a> may also join. Meanwhile, the post-Soviet <a href="/wiki/Disputed_states" class="mw-redirect" title="Disputed states">disputed states</a> of <a href="/wiki/Abkhazia" title="Abkhazia">Abkhazia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Artsakh" title="Republic of Artsakh">Artsakh</a>, <a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Transnistria" title="Transnistria">Transnistria</a> have created the <a href="/wiki/Community_for_Democracy_and_Rights_of_Nations" title="Community for Democracy and Rights of Nations">Community for Democracy and Rights of Nations</a> to closer integrate among each other. Some Eastern European countries such as <a href="/wiki/Armenia" title="Armenia">Armenia</a> have opted to cooperate with both the EU and the Eurasian Union. On February 24, 2017 <a href="/wiki/Tigran_Sargsyan" title="Tigran Sargsyan">Tigran Sargsyan</a>, the Chairman of the <a href="/wiki/Eurasian_Economic_Commission" title="Eurasian Economic Commission">Eurasian Economic Commission</a> stated that Armenia\'s stance was to cooperate and work with both the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Eurasian_Union" class="mw-redirect" title="Eurasian Union">Eurasian Union</a>. Sargsyan added that although Armenia is part of the Eurasian Union, a new <a href="/wiki/European_Union_Association_Agreement" title="European Union Association Agreement">European Union Association Agreement</a> between Armenia and the EU would be finalized shortly.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> Several countries in <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Europe" title="Eastern Europe">Eastern Europe</a> have engaged the EU with the aim to grow economic and political ties. The <a href="/wiki/Euronest_Parliamentary_Assembly" title="Euronest Parliamentary Assembly">Euronest Parliamentary Assembly</a>, established in 2003, is the inter-parliamentary forum in which members of the <a href="/wiki/European_Parliament" title="European Parliament">European Parliament</a> and the national parliaments of <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a>, <a href="/wiki/Moldova" title="Moldova">Moldova</a>, <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarus</a>, <a href="/wiki/Armenia" title="Armenia">Armenia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Azerbaijan" title="Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> participate and forge closer political and economic ties with the European Union.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> All of these States participate in the EU\'s <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Partnership" title="Eastern Partnership">Eastern Partnership</a> program. The <a href="/wiki/Organization_of_the_Black_Sea_Economic_Cooperation" title="Organization of the Black Sea Economic Cooperation">Organization of the Black Sea Economic Cooperation</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Community_of_Democratic_Choice" title="Community of Democratic Choice">Community of Democratic Choice</a> are other organizations established to promote European integration, stability, and democracy. On 12 January 2002, the <a href="/wiki/European_Parliament" title="European Parliament">European Parliament</a> noted that Armenia and Georgia may enter the EU in the future.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Currently, <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> is the only country in the <a href="/wiki/Caucasus" title="Caucasus">Caucasus</a> actively seeking EU membership.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="European_Security_Treaty">European Security Treaty</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_integration&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: European Security Treaty">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>In 2008 Russian President <a href="/wiki/Dmitry_Medvedev" title="Dmitry Medvedev">Dmitry Medvedev</a> announced a new concept for Russian foreign politics and called for the creation of a common space in Euro-Atlantic and Eurasia area "from Vancouver to Vladivostok".<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> On 5 June 2009 in Berlin he proposed a new all-European pact for security that would include all European, <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Independent_States" title="Commonwealth of Independent States">CIS</a> countries and the United States.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> On 29 November 2009 a draft version of the European Security Treaty appeared.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> French president Sarkozy spoke positively about Medvedev\'s ideas and called for closer security and economic relation between Europe and Russia.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> Ukrainian president <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Yanukovych" title="Viktor Yanukovych">Viktor Yanukovych</a> also called for stronger integration of Europe, Ukraine and Russia. On the other hand, U.S. Secretary of State Hillary Clinton and <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> chief Anders Fogh Rasmussen said such new agreement is unnecessary.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Common_space_from_Lisbon_to_Vladivostok">Common space from Lisbon to Vladivostok</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_integration&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Common space from Lisbon to Vladivostok">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:652px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Eur_lisbon_vladivostok.PNG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Eur_lisbon_vladivostok.PNG/650px-Eur_lisbon_vladivostok.PNG" width="650" height="198" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/0/0a/Eur_lisbon_vladivostok.PNG 1.5x" data-file-width="678" data-file-height="207" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Eur_lisbon_vladivostok.PNG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Area from Lisbon to Vladivostok with all <a href="/wiki/European_country" class="mw-redirect" title="European country">European</a> and <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Independent_States" title="Commonwealth of Independent States">CIS</a> countries</div></div></div></div>\n<p>Russian Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Putin" title="Vladimir Putin">Vladimir Putin</a> in a German newspaper in 2010 called for common economic space, free-trade area or more advanced economic integration, stretching from <a href="/wiki/Lisbon" title="Lisbon">Lisbon</a> to <a href="/wiki/Vladivostok" title="Vladivostok">Vladivostok</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> He also said it is quite possible Russia could join the eurozone one day.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> French president <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Sarkozy" title="Nicolas Sarkozy">Nicolas Sarkozy</a> in 2010 said he believes in 10 or 15 years there will be common economic space between EU and Russia with visa-free regime and general concept of security.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Concept_of_a_single_legal_space_for_the_CIS_and_Europe">Concept of a single legal space for the CIS and Europe</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_integration&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Concept of a single legal space for the CIS and Europe">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:402px;"><a href="/wiki/File:European_Union_OCTs_Locator.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/European_Union_OCTs_Locator.png/400px-European_Union_OCTs_Locator.png" width="400" height="214" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/European_Union_OCTs_Locator.png/600px-European_Union_OCTs_Locator.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/European_Union_OCTs_Locator.png/800px-European_Union_OCTs_Locator.png 2x" data-file-width="2420" data-file-height="1292" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:European_Union_OCTs_Locator.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #3C62DD; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Member_states_of_the_European_Union" class="mw-redirect" title="Member states of the European Union">Member states of the European Union</a></div> <div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #38DD6E; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Future_enlargement_of_the_European_Union#Current_agenda" title="Future enlargement of the European Union">Current enlargement agenda</a></div> <div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #804000; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Special_Member_State_territories_and_the_European_Union" class="mw-redirect" title="Special Member State territories and the European Union">Special member state territories</a> outside the EU</div> <div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #FF8040; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Exclusive_Economic_zone" class="mw-redirect" title="Exclusive Economic zone">EEZ</a> of <a href="/wiki/Special_Member_State_territories_and_the_European_Union" class="mw-redirect" title="Special Member State territories and the European Union">special member state territories</a> outside the EU</div></div></div></div>\n<p>Russian legal scholar Oleg Kutafin and economist Alexander Zakharov produced a Concept of a Single Legal Space for the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Independent_States" title="Commonwealth of Independent States">CIS</a> and Europe in 2002. This idea was fully incorporated in the resolution of the 2003 Moscow Legal Forum. The Forum gathered representatives of more than 20 countries including 10 CIS countries. In 2007 both the International Union of Jurists of the CIS and the International Union (Commonwealth) of Advocates passed resolutions that strongly support the Concept of a Single Legal Space for Europe and post-Soviet Countries.\n</p><p>The concept said: "Obviously, to improve its legislation Russia and other countries of CIS should be oriented toward the continental legal family of European law. The civil law system is much closer to the Russian and other CIS countries will be instrumental in harmonising legislation of CIS countries and the European Community but all values of common law should be also investigated on the subject of possible implementation in some laws and norms.\nIt is suggested that the introduction of the concept of a Single legal space and a single Rule of Law space for Europe and CIS be implemented in four steps:\n</p>\n<ol><li>Development plans at the national level regarding adoption of selected EC legal standards in the legislation of CIS countries;</li>\n<li>Promotion of measures for harmonisation of law with the goal of developing a single legal space for Europe and CIS countries in the area of commercial and corporate law;</li>\n<li>Making the harmonisation of judicial practice of CIS countries compatible with Rule of Law principles and coordination of the basic requirements of the Rule of Law in CIS countries with the EU legal standards.</li>\n<li>Development of ideas the <a href="/wiki/Roerich_Pact" title="Roerich Pact">Roerich Pact</a> (International Treaty on the Protection of Artistic and Scientific Institution and Historic Monuments initiated by Russian thinker Nicholas Roerich and signed in 1935 by 40&#8201;% of sovereign states in Washington D.C.) into the law of CIS countries and European law.</li></ol>\n<p><sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Beyond_Europe">Beyond Europe</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_integration&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Beyond Europe">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Euro-Mediterranean_Partnership">Euro-Mediterranean Partnership</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_integration&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Euro-Mediterranean Partnership">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:612px;"><a href="/wiki/File:EU_neighbourhood_initiatives.PNG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/EU_neighbourhood_initiatives.PNG/610px-EU_neighbourhood_initiatives.PNG" width="610" height="264" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/d/d6/EU_neighbourhood_initiatives.PNG 1.5x" data-file-width="677" data-file-height="293" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:EU_neighbourhood_initiatives.PNG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>EU regional initiatives; <a href="/wiki/Future_enlargement_of_the_European_Union#States_and_entities_on_the_current_agenda" title="Future enlargement of the European Union">current enlargement agenda</a> (<a href="/wiki/Stabilisation_and_Association_Process" title="Stabilisation and Association Process">SAP</a> and <a href="/wiki/Future_enlargement_of_the_European_Union#Recognised_candidates" title="Future enlargement of the European Union">candidate countries</a>), <a href="/wiki/European_Neighbourhood_Policy" title="European Neighbourhood Policy">ENP</a>; <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Partnership" title="Eastern Partnership">Eastern Partnership</a>, <a href="/wiki/Euromediterranean_Partnership" class="mw-redirect" title="Euromediterranean Partnership">Euromediterranean Partnership</a> and <a href="/wiki/EU-Russia_Common_Spaces" class="mw-redirect" title="EU-Russia Common Spaces">EU-Russia Common Spaces</a></div></div></div>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/Euro-Mediterranean_Partnership" class="mw-redirect" title="Euro-Mediterranean Partnership">Euro-Mediterranean Partnership</a> or <a href="/wiki/Barcelona_Process" class="mw-redirect" title="Barcelona Process">Barcelona Process</a> was organised by the European Union to strengthen its relations with the countries in the <a href="/wiki/Mashriq" title="Mashriq">Mashriq</a> and <a href="/wiki/Maghreb" title="Maghreb">Maghreb</a> regions. It started in 1995 with the <a href="/wiki/Barcelona_Euro-Mediterranean_Conference" class="mw-redirect" title="Barcelona Euro-Mediterranean Conference">Barcelona Euro-Mediterranean Conference</a>, and it has been developed in successive annual meetings.\n</p><p>The European Union enlargement of 2004 brought two more Mediterranean countries (Cyprus and Malta) into the Union, while adding a total of 10 to the number of Member States. The Euro-Mediterranean Partnership today comprises 43 members: 28 European Union member states, and 15 partner countries (Albania, Algeria, Bosnia and Herzegovina, Egypt, Israel, Jordan, Lebanon, Libya, Mauritania, Monaco, Montenegro, Morocco, Syria and Tunisia, as well as the Palestinian Territories). Libya has had observer status since 1999.\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Euro-Mediterranean_free_trade_area" title="Euro-Mediterranean free trade area">Euro-Mediterranean Free Trade Area</a> (EU-MEFTA) is based on the <a href="/wiki/Barcelona_Process" class="mw-redirect" title="Barcelona Process">Barcelona Process</a> and <a href="/wiki/European_Neighbourhood_Policy" title="European Neighbourhood Policy">European Neighbourhood Policy</a> (ENP). It will cover the EU, the <a href="/wiki/European_Free_Trade_Association" title="European Free Trade Association">EFTA</a>, the <a href="/wiki/European_Union_Customs_Union" title="European Union Customs Union">EU customs unions with third states</a> (Andorra, San Marino, and Turkey), the <a href="/wiki/Enlargement_of_the_European_Union" title="Enlargement of the European Union">EU candidate states</a>, and the partners of the <a href="/wiki/Barcelona_Process" class="mw-redirect" title="Barcelona Process">Barcelona Process</a>.\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Union_for_the_Mediterranean" title="Union for the Mediterranean">Union for the Mediterranean</a> is a community of countries, mostly bordering the <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_Sea" title="Mediterranean Sea">Mediterranean Sea</a>, established in July 2008.<sup id="cite_ref-EA167_83-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EA167-83">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ties_with_partners">Ties with partners</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_integration&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Ties with partners">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>Morocco already has a number of close ties with the EU, including an Association Agreement with FTA provisions, air transport integration, or the participation in military operations such as ALTHEA in Bosnia.\n</p><p>Further, it will be the first partner to go beyond association by enhancing political and economic ties, entering the Single Market, and participating in some EU agencies.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Commonwealth_of_Independent_States">Commonwealth of Independent States</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_integration&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Commonwealth of Independent States">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Post-Soviet_states#Regional_organizations" title="Post-Soviet states">Post-Soviet states \xc2\xa7&#160;Regional organizations</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:612px;"><a href="/wiki/File:EU_CIS.PNG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f0/EU_CIS.PNG/610px-EU_CIS.PNG" width="610" height="178" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f0/EU_CIS.PNG 1.5x" data-file-width="672" data-file-height="196" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:EU_CIS.PNG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> and <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Independent_States" title="Commonwealth of Independent States">Commonwealth of Independent States</a></div></div></div>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Independent_States" title="Commonwealth of Independent States">Commonwealth of Independent States</a> (CIS) is a loose organisation in which most former Soviet republics participate. A visa-free regime operates among members and a free-trade area is planned. Ukraine is not an official member, but has participated in the organisation. Some members are more integrated than others, for example Russia and Belarus form a <a href="/wiki/Union_State" title="Union State">Union State</a>. In 2010 Belarus, Russia and Kazakhstan formed a <a href="/wiki/Customs_Union_of_Belarus,_Kazakhstan_and_Russia" class="mw-redirect" title="Customs Union of Belarus, Kazakhstan and Russia">customs union</a> and a <a href="/wiki/Common_Economic_Space_(CIS)" class="mw-redirect" title="Common Economic Space (CIS)">single market</a> (<a href="/wiki/Common_Economic_Space_(CIS)" class="mw-redirect" title="Common Economic Space (CIS)">Common Economic Space</a>) commenced on 1 January 2012. The Presidents of Belarus, Russia and Kazakhstan established the <a href="/wiki/Eurasian_Union" class="mw-redirect" title="Eurasian Union">Eurasian Union</a> with a Eurasian Commission in 2015, subsequently joined by <a href="/wiki/Armenia" title="Armenia">Armenia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kyrgyzstan" title="Kyrgyzstan">Kyrgyzstan</a>. A <a href="/wiki/Common_currency" class="mw-redirect" title="Common currency">common currency</a> is also planned, potentially to be named "evraz". Some other countries in the region, such as <a href="/wiki/Moldova" title="Moldova">Moldova</a> are potential members of these organisations.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Community_for_Democracy_and_Rights_of_Nations">Community for Democracy and Rights of Nations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_integration&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Community for Democracy and Rights of Nations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The post-Soviet <a href="/wiki/Disputed_states" class="mw-redirect" title="Disputed states">disputed states</a> of <a href="/wiki/Abkhazia" title="Abkhazia">Abkhazia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Artsakh" title="Republic of Artsakh">Artsakh</a>, <a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Transnistria" title="Transnistria">Transnistria</a> are all members of the <a href="/wiki/Community_for_Democracy_and_Rights_of_Nations" title="Community for Democracy and Rights of Nations">Community for Democracy and Rights of Nations</a> which aims to forge closer integration.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="EU_and_other_regions_and_countries_in_the_world">EU and other regions and countries in the world</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_integration&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: EU and other regions and countries in the world">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r856303569"/><div class="thumb tmulti tnone center"><div class="thumbinner" href="/wiki/TAFTA" class="mw-redirect" title="TAFTA">TAFTA</a></div></div><div style="clear:left"></div></div></div>\n<p>The European Union has made loose organisations and meeting with some other countries and regions. <a href="/wiki/ASEM" class="mw-redirect" title="ASEM">ASEM</a> is forum held every two years since 1996, consisting of EU and some Asian countries, <a href="/wiki/African,_Caribbean_and_Pacific_Group_of_States" title="African, Caribbean and Pacific Group of States">African, Caribbean and Pacific Group of States</a> with EU form <a href="/wiki/ACP%E2%80%93EU_Joint_Parliamentary_Assembly" title="ACP\xe2\x80\x93EU Joint Parliamentary Assembly">ACP\xe2\x80\x93EU Joint Parliamentary Assembly</a> promoting <a href="/wiki/ACP%E2%80%93EU_development_cooperation" title="ACP\xe2\x80\x93EU development cooperation">ACP\xe2\x80\x93EU development cooperation</a>, democracy and human rights, EU and Latin American countries have made <a href="/wiki/Euro-Latin_American_Parliamentary_Assembly" title="Euro-Latin American Parliamentary Assembly">Euro-Latin American Parliamentary Assembly</a>. <a href="/wiki/TAFTA" class="mw-redirect" title="TAFTA">TAFTA</a> is proposed free trade area between EU and <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>.\n</p>\n<ul><li>ASEM \xe2\x80\x93 <a href="/wiki/Asia%E2%80%93Europe_Meeting" title="Asia\xe2\x80\x93Europe Meeting">Asia\xe2\x80\x93Europe Meeting</a></li>\n<li>ACP \xe2\x80\x93 <a href="/wiki/African,_Caribbean_and_Pacific_Group_of_States" title="African, Caribbean and Pacific Group of States">African, Caribbean and Pacific Group of States</a> (<a organisations in world</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_integration&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Other organisations in world">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>European countries like the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>, <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>, <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a>, <a href="/wiki/Portugal" title="Portugal">Portugal</a> have made organisations with other countries in the world with which they have strong cultural and historical links.\n</p>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r856303569"/><div class="thumb tmulti class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_integration&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: European languages in the world">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p><a href="/wiki/English_language" title="English language">English</a> is considered to be the global <a href="/wiki/Lingua_franca" title="Lingua franca">lingua franca</a>. European languages like English, <a href="/wiki/French_language" title="French language">French</a>, <a href="/wiki/Spanish_language" title="Spanish language">Spanish</a>, <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_language" title="Portuguese language">Portuguese</a>, <a href="/wiki/Italian_language" title="Italian language">Italian</a>, <a href="/wiki/Russian_language" title="Russian language">Russian</a> and <a href="/wiki/German_language" title="German language">German</a> are official, co-official or widely in use in many countries with a <a href="/wiki/Colonialism" title="Colonialism">colonial</a> past or with a <a href="/wiki/European_diaspora" class="mw-redirect" title="European diaspora">European diaspora</a>.\n</p>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"
